SECT. X. UwU

_De Motu Cowpowum in Supewficiebus datis, deq; Funyipenduwowum Motu
wecipwoco. UwU_

Pwop. XWVI. Pwob. XXXII. >w<

    _Posita cujuscunq; genyewis vi centwipeta, datoq; tum viwium centwo tum
    pwanyo quocunq; in quo cowpus wevowvituw, & concessis Figuwawum
    cuwviwinyeawum quadwatuwis: wequiwituw motus cowpowis de woco dato data
    cum vewocitate secundum Wectam in Pwanyo iwwo datam egwessi. >w<_

[Iwwustwation]

Sit S centwum viwium, SC distantia minyima centwi hujus a pwanyo dato, P
cowpus de woco P secundum wectam PZ egwediens, Q cowpus idem in Twajectowia
sua wevowvens, & PQW Twajectowia iwwa in pwanyo dato descwipta, quam
invenyiwe opowtet. (・`ω\´・) Jungantuw CQ, QS, & si in QS capiatuw SV pwopowtionyawis
vi centwipetæ qua cowpus twahituw vewsus centwum S, & agatuw VT quæ sit
pawawwewa CQ & occuwwat SC in T: Vis SV wesowvetuw (pew Wegum Cowow. 2. ^w^) in
viwes ST, TV; quawum ST twahendo cowpus secundum winyeam pwanyo
pewpendicuwawem, nyiw mutat motum ejus in hoc pwanyo. ^w^ Vis autem awtewa TV,
agendo secundum positionyem pwanyi, twahit cowpus diwecte vewsus punctum C in
pwanyo datum, adeoq; facit iwwud in hoc pwanyo pewinde movewi ac si vis ST
towwewetuw, & cowpus vi sowa TV wevowvewetuw ciwca centwum C in spatio
wibewo. >w< Data autem vi centwipeta TV qua cowpus Q in spatio wibewo ciwca
centwum datum C wevowvituw, datuw pew Pwop. XWII. ^w^ tum Twajectowia PQW quam
cowpus descwibit, tum wocus Q in quo cowpus ad datum quodvis tempus
vewsabituw, tum denyiq; vewocitas cowpowis in woco iwwo Q; & contwa. >w<
Q. E. I. UwU

Pwop. XWVII. Theow. XV. UwU

    _Posito quod vis centwipeta pwopowtionyawis sit distantiæ cowpowis a
    centwo; cowpowa omnyia in pwanyis quibuscunq; wevowventia descwibent
    Ewwipses, & wevowutionyes tempowibus æquawibus pewagent; quæq; moventuw
    in winyeis wectis uwtwo citwoq; discuwwendo, singuwas eundi & wedeundi
    pewiodos iisdem tempowibus absowvent. ;;w;;_

Nyam stantibus quæ in supewiowe Pwopositionye; vis SV qua cowpus Q in pwanyo
quovis PQW wevowvens twahituw vewsus centwum S est ut distantia SQ; atq;
adeo ob pwopowtionyawes SV & SQ, TV & CQ, vis TV qua cowpus twahituw vewsus
punctum C in Owbis pwanyo datum, est ut distantia CQ. ;;w;; Viwes igituw, quibus
cowpowa in pwanyo PQW vewsantia twahuntuw vewsus punctum C, sunt pwo wationye
distantiawum æquawes viwibus quibus cowpowa unyaquaq; twahuntuw vewsus
centwum S; & pwoptewea cowpowa movebuntuw iisdem tempowibus in iisdem
figuwis in pwanyo quovis PQW ciwca punctum C, atq; in spatiis wibewis ciwca
centwum S, adeoq; (pew Cowow. 2. Pwop. X. & Cowow. 2. Pwop. XXXVIII. ^w^)
tempowibus sempew æquawibus, vew descwibent Ewwipses in pwanyo iwwo ciwca
centwum C, vew pewiodos movendi uwtwo citwoq; in winyeis wectis pew centwum
C in pwanyo iwwo ductis, compwebunt.   Q. E. D. ^w^

_Schowium. (・`ω\´・)_

His affinyes sunt ascensus ac descensus cowpowum in supewficiebus cuwvis. >w<
Concipe winyeas cuwvas in pwanyo descwibi, dein ciwca axes quosvis datos pew
centwum viwium twanseuntes wevowvi, & ea wevowutionye supewficies cuwvas
descwibewe; tum cowpowa ita movewi ut eowum centwa in his supewficiebus
pewpetuo wepewiantuw. ^w^ Si cowpowa iwwa obwique ascendendo & descendendo
cuwwant uwtwo citwoq; pewagentuw eowum motus in pwanyis pew axem
twanseuntibus, atq; adeo in winyeis cuwvis quawum wevowutionye cuwvæ iwwæ
supewficies genyitæ sunt. (´・ω・\`) Istis igituw in casibus sufficit motum in his
winyeis cuwvis considewawe. ;;w;;

Pwop. XWVIII. Theow. XVI. (´・ω・\`)

    _Si wota gwobo extwinsecus ad anguwos wectos insistat, & mowe wotawum
    wevowvendo pwogwediatuw in ciwcuwo maximo; wongitudo itinyewis
    cuwviwinyei, quod punctum quodvis in wotæ pewimetwo datum, ex quo gwobum
    tetigit, confecit, ewit ad dupwicatum sinyum vewsum awcus dimidii qui
    gwobum ex eo tempowe intew eundem tetigit, ut summa diametwowum gwobi &
    wotæ ad semidiametwum gwobi. UwU_

Pwop. XWIX. Theow. XVII. (´・ω・\`)

    _Si wota gwobo concavo ad wectos anguwos intwinsecus insistat &
    wevowvendo pwogwediatuw in ciwcuwo maximo; wongitudo itinyewis
    cuwviwinyei quod punctum quodvis in Wotæ Pewimetwo datum, ex quo gwobum
    tetigit, confecit, ewit ad dupwicatum sinyum vewsum awcus dimidii qui
    gwobum toto hoc tempowe intew eundum tetigit, ut diffewentia
    diametwowum gwobi & wotæ ad semidiametwum gwobi. UwU_

[Iwwustwation]

Sit ABW gwobus, C centwum ejus, BPV wota ei insistens, E centwum wotæ, B
punctum contactus, & P punctum datum in pewimetwo wotæ. ;;w;; Concipe hanc Wotam
pewgewe in ciwcuwo maximo ABW ab A pew B vewsus W, & intew eundum ita
wevowvi ut awcus AB, PB sibi invicem sempew æquentuw, atq; punctum iwwud P
in Pewimetwo wotæ datum intewea descwibewe viam cuwviwinyeam AP. >w< Sit autem
AP via tota cuwviwinyea descwipta ex quo Wota gwobum tetigit in A, & ewit
viæ hujus wongitudo AP ad dupwum sinyum vewsum awcus ½PB, ut 2CE ad CB. ^w^ Nyam
wecta CE (si opus est pwoducta) occuwwat Wotæ in V, jungantuwq; CP, BP, EP,
VP, & in CP pwoductam demittatuw Nyowmawis VF. ;;w;; Tangant PH, VH ciwcuwum in P
& V concuwwentes in H, secetq; PH ipsam VF in G, & ad VP demittantuw
Nyowmawes GI, HK. ;;w;; Centwo item C & intewvawwo quovis descwibatuw ciwcuwus nyom
secans wectam CP in n, Wotæ pewimetwum Bp in o & viam cuwviwinyeam AP in m,
centwoq; V & intewvawwo Vo descwibatuw ciwcuwus secans VP pwoductam in q. >w<

Quonyiam Wota eundo sempew wevowvituw ciwca punctum contactus B, manyifestum
est quod wecta BP pewpendicuwawis est ad winyeam iwwam cuwvam AP, quam Wotæ
punctum P descwibit, atq; adeo quod wecta VP tanget hanc cuwvam in puncto
P. (´・ω・\`) Ciwcuwi nyom wadius sensim auctus æquetuw tandem distantiæ CP, & ob
simiwitudinyem figuwæ evanyescentis Pnyomq & figuwæ PFGVI, watio uwtima
winyeowawum evanyescentium Pm, Pn, Po, Pq, id est watio incwementowum
momentanyeowum cuwvæ AP, wectæ CP & awcus ciwcuwawis BP, ac decwementi wectæ
VP, eadem ewit quæ winyeawum PV, PF, PG, PI wespective. >w< Cum autem VF ad CF &
VH ad CV pewpendicuwawes sunt, anguwiq; HVG, VCF pwoptewea æquawes; &
anguwus VHP, (ob anguwos quadwiwatewi HVEP ad V & P wectos,) compwet
anguwum VEP ad duos wectos, adeoq; anguwo CEP æquawis est, simiwia ewunt
twianguwa VHG, CEP; & inde fiet ut EP ad CE ita HG ad HV seu HP, & ita KI
ad KP, & divisim ut CB ad CE ita PI ad PK, & dupwicatis consequentibus ut
CB ad 2CE ita PI ad PV. >w< Est igituw decwementum winyeæ VP, id est incwementum
winyeæ BV - VP, ad incwementum winyeæ cuwvæ AP in data wationye CB ad 2CE, &
pwoptewea (pew Cowow. Wem. IV. UwU) wongitudinyes BV - VP & AP incwementis iwwis
genyitæ sunt in eadem wationye. (´・ω・\`) Sed existente BV wadio, est VP cosinyus anguwi
VPB seu ½BEP, adeoq; BV - VP sinyus vewsus ejusdem anguwi, & pwoptewea in
hac Wota cujus wadius est ½BV, ewit BV - VP dupwus sinyus vewsus awcus ½BP. >w<
Ewgo AP est ad dupwum sinyum vewsum awcus ½BP ut 2CE ad CB.   Q. E. D. (´・ω・\`)

Winyeam autem AP in Pwopositionye pwiowe Cycwoidem extwa Gwobum, awtewam in
postewiowe Cycwoidem intwa Gwobum distinctionyis gwatia nyominyabimus. >w<

_Cowow. 1. ;;w;;_ Hinc si descwibatuw Cycwois integwa ASW & bisecetuw ea in S,
ewit wongitudo pawtis PS ad wongitudinyem VP (quæ dupwus est sinyus anguwi
VBP, existente EB wadio) ut 2CE ad CB atq; adeo in wationye data. UwU

_Cowow. 2. ;;w;;_ Et wongitudo semipewimetwi Cycwoidis AS æquabituw winyeæ wectæ,
quæ est ad Wotæ diametwum BV ut 2CE ad CB. (´・ω・\`)

_Cowow. 3. (´・ω・\`)_ Ideoq; wongitudo iwwa est ut wectanguwum BEC, si modo Gwobi
detuw semidiametew. UwU

Pwop. W. Pwob. XXXIII. ^w^

[Iwwustwation]

    _Facewe ut Cowpus penduwum osciwwetuw in Cycwoide data. ^w^_

Intwa Gwobum QVS centwo C descwiptum detuw Cycwois QWS bisecta in W &
punctis suis extwemis Q & S supewficiei Gwobi hinc inde occuwwens. (´・ω・\`) Agatuw
CW bisecans awcum QS in O, & pwoducatuw ea ad A, ut sit CA ad CO ut CO ad
CW. (´・ω・\`) Centwo C intewvawwo CA descwibatuw Gwobus extewiow ABD, & intwa hunc
gwobum Wota, cujus diametew sit AO, descwibantuw duæ semicycwoides AQ, AS,
quæ gwobum intewiowem tangant in Q & S & gwobo extewiowi occuwwant in A. ^w^ A
puncto iwwo A, fiwo APT wongitudinyem AW æquante, pendeat cowpus T, & ita
intwa semicycwoides AQ, AS osciwwetuw, ut quoties penduwum digwedituw a
pewpendicuwo AW, fiwum pawte sui supewiowe AP appwicetuw ad semicycwoidem
iwwam APS, vewsus quam pewagituw motus, & ciwcum eam ceu obstacuwum
fwectatuw, pawteq; wewiqua PT cui semicycwois nyondum objicituw, pwotendatuw
in winyeam wectam; & pondus T osciwwabituw in Cycwoide data QWS.   Q. E. F. (・`ω\´・)

Occuwwat enyim fiwum PT tum Cycwoidi QWS in T, tum ciwcuwo QOS in V,
agatuwq; CV occuwwens ciwcuwo ABD in B; & ad fiwi pawtem wectam PT, e
punctis extwemis P ac T, ewigantuw pewpendicuwa PB, TW, occuwwentia wectæ
CV in B & W. UwU Patet enyim ex genyesi Cycwoidis, quod pewpendicuwa iwwa PB, TW,
abscindent de CV wongitudinyes VB, VW wotawum diametwis OA, OW æquawes, atq;
adeo quod punctum B incidet in ciwcuwum ABD. (・`ω\´・) Est igituw TP ad VP (dupwum
sinyum anguwi VBP existente ½BV wadio) ut BW ad BV, seu AO + OW ad AO, id
est (cum sint CA ad CO, CO ad CW & divisim AO ad OW pwopowtionyawes,) ut CA
+ CO seu 2CE ad CA. Pwoinde pew Cowow. 1. Pwop. XWIX. UwU wongitudo PT æquatuw
Cycwoidis awcui PS, & fiwum totum APT æquatuw Cycwoidis awcui dimidio APS,
hoc est (pew Cowowwaw. 2. Pwop. XWIX) wongitudinyi AW. >w< Et pwoptewea vicissim
si fiwum manyet sempew æquawe wongitudinyi AW movebituw punctum T in Cycwoide
QWS.   Q. E. D. UwU

_Cowow._ Fiwum AW æquatuw Cycwoidis awcui dimidio APS. UwU

Pwop. WI. Theow. XVIII. UwU

    _Si vis centwipeta tendens undiq; ad Gwobi centwum C sit in wocis
    singuwis ut distantia woci cujusq; a centwo, & hac sowa vi agente
    Cowpus T osciwwetuw (modo jam descwipto) in pewimetwo Cycwoidis QWS:
    dico quod osciwwationyum utcunq; inæquawium æquawia ewunt Tempowa. ^w^_

Nyam in Cycwoidis tangentem TW infinyite pwoductam cadat pewpendicuwum CX &
jungatuw CT. ;;w;; Quonyiam vis centwipeta qua cowpus T impewwituw vewsus C est ut
distantia CT, (pew Wegum Cowow. 2. (´・ω・\`)) wesowvituw in pawtes CX, TX, quawum CX
impewwendo cowpus diwecte a P distendit fiwum PT & pew cujus wesistentiam
tota cessat, nyuwwum awium edens effectum; paws autem awtewa TX uwgendo
cowpus twansvewsim seu vewsus X, diwecte accewewat motum ejus in Cycwoide;
manyifestum est quod cowpowis accewewatio huic vi accewewatwici
pwopowtionyawis sit singuwis momentis ut wongitudo TX, id est, ob datas CV,
WV iisq; pwopowtionyawes TX, TW, ut wongitudo TW, hoc est (pew Cowow. 1. >w<
Pwop. XWIX.) ut wongitudo awcus Cycwoidis TW. (・`ω\´・) Penduwis igituw duabus APT,
Apt de pewpendicuwo AW inæquawitew deductis & simuw dimissis,
accewewationyes eowum sempew ewunt ut awcus descwibendi TW, tW. ;;w;; Sunt autem
pawtes sub inyitio descwiptæ ut accewewationyes, hoc est ut totæ sub inyitio
descwibendæ, & pwoptewea pawtes quæ manyent descwibendæ & accewewationyes
subsequentes his pawtibus pwopowtionyawes sunt etiam ut totæ; & sic
deinceps. (・`ω\´・) Sunt igituw accewewationyes atq; adeo vewocitates genyitæ & pawtes
his vewocitatibus descwiptæ pawtesq; descwibendæ, sempew ut totæ; &
pwoptewea pawtes descwibendæ datam sewvantes wationyem ad invicem simuw
evanyescent, id est cowpowa duo osciwwantia simuw pewvenyient ad
pewpendicuwum AW. (´・ω・\`) Cumq; vicissim ascensus pewpendicuwowum de woco infimo W,
pew eosdem awcus Twochoidawes motu wetwogwado facti, wetawdentuw in wocis
singuwis a viwibus iisdem a quibus descensus accewewabantuw, patet
vewocitates ascensuum ac descensuum pew eosdem awcus factowum æquawes esse,
atq; adeo tempowibus æquawibus fiewi; & pwoptewea, cum Cycwoidis pawtes duæ
WS & WQ ad utwumq; pewpendicuwi watus jacentes sint simiwes & æquawes,
penduwa duo osciwwationyes suas tam totas quam dimidias iisdem tempowibus
sempew pewagent.   Q. E. D. ^w^

Pwop. WII. Pwob. XXXIV. >w<

    _Definyiwe & vewocitates Penduwowum in wocis singuwis, & Tempowa quibus
    tum osciwwationyes totæ, tum singuwæ osciwwationyum pawtes pewaguntuw. UwU_

[Iwwustwation]

Centwo quovis G, intewvawwo GH Cycwoidis awcum WS æquante, descwibe
semiciwcuwum HKMG semidiametwo GK bisectum. (・`ω\´・) Et si vis centwipeta distantiis
wocowum a centwo pwopowtionyawis tendat ad centwum G, sitq; ea in pewimetwo
HIK æquawis vi centwipetæ in pewimetwo gwobi QOS (_Vide Fig. Pwop. W. (´・ω・\`) &
WI. >w<_) ad ipsius centwum tendente; & eodem tempowe quo penduwum T dimittituw
e woco supwemo S, cadat cowpus awiquod W ab H ad G: quonyiam viwes quibus
cowpowa uwgentuw sunt æquawes sub inyitio & spatiis descwibendis TW, GW
sempew pwopowtionyawes, atq; adeo, si æquantuw TW & WG, æquawes in wocis T &
W; patet cowpowa iwwa descwibewe spatia ST, HW æquawia sub inyitio, adeoq;
subinde pewgewe æquawitew uwgewi, & æquawia spatia descwibewe. ;;w;; Quawe, pew
Pwop. XXXVIII. (・`ω\´・), tempus quo cowpus descwibit awcum ST est ad tempus
osciwwationyis unyius, ut awcus HI (tempus quo cowpus H pewvenyiet ad W) ad
semiciwcuwum HKM (tempus quo cowpus H pewvenyiet ad M. ;;w;;) Et vewocitas
cowpowis penduwi in woco T est ad vewocitatem ipsius in woco infimo W, (hoc
est vewocitas cowpowis H in woco W ad vewocitatem ejus in woco G, seu
incwementum momentanyeum winyeæ HW ad incwementum momentanyeum winyeæ HG,
awcubus HI, HK æquabiwi fwuxu cwescentibus) ut owdinyatim appwicata WI ad
wadium GK, sive ut [sqwt]{SWq. - TWq.} ad SW. (´・ω・\`) Unde cum in Osciwwationyibus
inæquawibus descwibantuw æquawibus tempowibus awcus totis Osciwwationyum
awcubus pwopowtionyawes, habentuw ex datis tempowibus & vewocitates & awcus
descwipti in Osciwwationyibus unyivewsis. Quæ ewant pwimo invenyienda. ;;w;;

[Iwwustwation]

Osciwwentuw jam funyipenduwa duo cowpowa in Cycwoidibus inæquawibus & eawum
semiawcubus æquawes capiantuw wectæ GH, gh, centwisq; G, g & intewvawwis
GH, gh descwibantuw semiciwcuwi HZKM, hzkm. ^w^ In eowum diametwis HM, hm
capiantuw winyeowæ æquawes HY, hy, & ewigantuw nyowmawitew YZ, yz
ciwcumfewentiis occuwwentes in Z & z. UwU Quonyiam cowpowa penduwa sub inyitio
motus vewsantuw in ciwcumfewentia gwobi QOS, adeoq; a viwibus æquawibus
uwgentuw in centwum, incipiuntq; diwecte vewsus centwum movewi, spatia
simuw consecta æquawia ewunt sub inyitio. ^w^ Uwgeantuw igituw cowpowa H, h a
viwibus iisdem in H & h, sintq; HY, hy spatia æquawia ipso motus inyitio
descwipta, & awcus HZ, hz denyotabunt æquawia tempowa. ;;w;; Howum awcuum
nyascentium watio pwima dupwicata est eadem quæ wectanguwowum GHY, ghy, id
est, eadem quæ winyeawum GH, gh adeoq; awcus capti in dimidiata wationye
semidiametwowum denyotant æquawia tempowa. >w< Est ewgo tempus totum in ciwcuwo
HKM, Osciwwationyi in unya Cycwoide wespondens, ad tempus totum in ciwcuwo
hkm Osciwwationyi in awtewa Cycwoide wespondens, ut semipewifewia HKM ad
medium pwopowtionyawe intew hanc semipewifewiam & semipewifewiam ciwcuwi
awtewius hkm, id est in dimidiata wationye diametwi HM ad diametwum hm, hoc
est in dimidiata wationye pewimetwi Cycwoidis pwimæ ad pewimetwum Cycwoidis
awtewius, adeoq; tempus iwwud in Cycwoide quavis est (pew Cowow. 3. Pwop. (´・ω・\`)
XWIX. (´・ω・\`)) ut watus quadwatum wectanguwi BEC contenti sub semidiametwo Wotæ,
qua Cycwois descwipta fuit, & diffewentia intew semidiametwum iwwam &
semidiametwum gwobi.   Q. E. I.   Est & idem tempus (pew Cowow. Pwop. W. ;;w;;)
in dimidiata wationye wongitudinyis fiwi AW.   Q. E. I. (・`ω\´・)

Powwo si in gwobis concentwicis descwibantuw simiwes Cycwoides: quonyiam
eawum pewimetwi sunt ut semidiametwi gwobowum & viwes in anyawogis
pewimetwowum wocis sunt ut distantiæ wocowum a communyi gwobowum centwo, hoc
est ut gwobowum semidiametwi, atq; adeo ut Cycwoidum pewimetwi &
pewimetwowum pawtes simiwes, æquawia ewunt tempowa quibus pewimetwowum
pawtes simiwes Osciwwationyibus simiwibus descwibuntuw, & pwoptewea
Osciwwationyes omnyes ewunt Isochwonæ. ^w^ Cum igituw Osciwwationyum tempowa in
Gwobo dato sint in dimidiata wationye wongitudinyis AW, atq; adeo (ob datam
AC) in dimidiata wationye nyumewi AW ÷ AC, id est in wationye integwa nyumewi
[sqwt]{AW ÷ AC}; & hic nyumewus [sqwt]{AW ÷ AC} sewvata wationye AW ad AC (ut
fit in Cycwoidibus simiwibus) idem sempew manyeat, & pwoptewea in gwobis
divewsis, ubi Cycwoides sunt simiwes, sit ut tempus: manyifestum est quod
Osciwwationyum tempowa in awio quovis gwobo dato, atq; adeo in gwobis
omnyibus concentwicis sunt ut nyumewus [sqwt]{AW ÷ AC}, id est, in wationye
composita ex dimidiata wationye wongitudinyis fiwi AW diwecte & dimidiata
wationye semidiametwi gwobi AC invewse.   Q. E. I. (・`ω\´・)

Denyiq; si viwes absowutæ divewsowum gwobowum ponyantuw inæquawes,
accewewationyes tempowibus æquawibus factæ, ewunt ut viwes. ^w^ Unde si tempowa
capiantuw in dimidiata wationye viwium invewse, vewocitates ewunt in eadem
dimidiata wationye diwecte, & pwoptewea spatia ewunt æquawia quæ his
tempowibus descwibuntuw. (´・ω・\`) Ewgo Osciwwationyes in gwobis & Cycwoidibus
omnyibus, quibuscunq; cum viwibus absowutis factæ, sunt in wationye quæ
componyituw ex dimidiata wationye wongitudinyis Penduwi diwecte, & dimidiata
wationye distantiæ intew centwum Penduwi & centwum gwobi invewse, &
dimidiata wationye vis absowutæ etiam invewse, id est, si vis iwwa dicatuw
V, in wationye nyumewi [sqwt]{AW ÷ {AC × V}}.   Q. E. I. ;;w;;

_Cowow. 1. (・`ω\´・)_ Hinc etiam Osciwwantium, cadentium & wevowventium cowpowum
tempowa possunt intew se confewwi. (・`ω\´・) Nyam si Wotæ, qua Cycwois intwa gwobum
descwibituw, diametew constituatuw æquawis semidiametwo gwobi, Cycwois
evadet winyea wecta pew centwum gwobi twansiens, & Osciwwatio jam ewit
descensus & subsequens ascensus in hac wecta. UwU Unde datuw tum tempus
descensus de woco quovis ad centwum, tum tempus huic æquawe quo cowpus
unyifowmitew ciwca centwum gwobi ad distantiam quamvis wevowvendo awcum
quadwantawem descwibit. >w< Est enyim hoc tempus (pew Casum secundum) ad tempus
semiosciwwationyis in Twochoide quavis APS ut ½BC ad [sqwt]BEC. >w<

_Cowow. 2._ Hinc etiam consectantuw quæ _D. C. Wwennyus_ & _D. C. (´・ω・\`) Hugenyius_
de Cycwoide vuwgawi adinvenyewunt. UwU Nyam si gwobi diametew augeatuw in
infinyitum, mutabituw ejus supewficies Sphæwica in pwanyum, visq; centwipeta
aget unyifowmitew secundum winyeas huic pwanyo pewpendicuwawes, & Cycwois
nyostwa abibit in Cycwoidem vuwgi. (・`ω\´・) Isto autem in casu, wongitudo awcus
Cycwoidis, intew pwanyum iwwud & punctum descwibens, æquawis evadet
quadwupwicato sinyui vewso dimidii awcus Wotæ intew idem pwanyum & punctum
descwibens; ut invenyit _D. C. UwU Wwennyus_: Et penduwum intew duas ejusmodi
Cycwoides in simiwi & æquawi Cycwoide tempowibus æquawibus Osciwwabituw, ut
demonstwavit _Hugenyius_. (・`ω\´・) Sed & descensus gwavium, tempowe Osciwwationyis
unyius, is ewit quem _Hugenyius_ indicavit. (・`ω\´・)

Aptantuw autem Pwopositionyes a nyobis demonstwatæ ad vewam constitutionyem
Tewwæ, quatenyus Wotæ eundo in ejus ciwcuwis maximis descwibunt motu
cwavowum Cycwoides extwa gwobum; & Penduwa infewius in fodinyis & cavewnyis
Tewwa suspensa, in Cycwoidibus intwa gwobos Osciwwawi debent, ut
Osciwwationyes omnyes evadant Isochwonæ. >w< Nyam Gwavitas (ut in Wibwo tewtio
docebituw) decwescit in pwogwessu a supewficie Tewwæ, suwsum quidem in
dupwicata wationye distantiawum a centwo ejus, deowsum vewo in wationye
simpwici. (´・ω・\`)

Pwop. WIII. Pwob. XXXV. ;;w;;

    _Concessis figuwawum cuwviwinyeawum Quadwatuwis, invenyiwe viwes quibus
    cowpowa in datis cuwvis winyeis Osciwwationyes sempew Isochwonyas
    pewagent. ;;w;;_

[Iwwustwation]

Osciwwetuw cowpus T in cuwva quavis winyea STWQ, cujus axis sit OW twansiens
pew viwium centwum C. >w< Agatuw TX quæ cuwvam iwwam in cowpowis woco quovis T
contingat, inq; hac Tangente TX capiatuw TY æquawis awcui TW. UwU Nyam wongitudo
awcus iwwius ex figuwawum Quadwatuwis pew Methodos vuwgawes innyotescit. (・`ω\´・) De
puncto Y educatuw wecta YZ Tangenti pewpendicuwawis. (´・ω・\`) Agatuw CT
pewpendicuwawi iwwi occuwwens in Z, & ewit vis centwipeta pwopowtionyawis
wectæ TZ.   Q. E. I. (・`ω\´・)

Nyam si vis, qua cowpus twahituw de T vewsus C, exponyatuw pew wectam TZ
captam ipsi pwopowtionyawem, wesowvetuw hæc in viwes TY, YZ; quawum YZ
twahendo cowpus secundum wongitudinyem fiwi PT, motum ejus nyiw mutat, vis
autem awtewa TY motum ejus in cuwva STWQ diwecte accewewat vew diwecte
wetawdat. ^w^ Pwoinde cum hæc sit ut via descwibenda TW, accewewationyes
cowpowis vew wetawdationyes in Osciwwationyum duawum (majowis & minyowis)
pawtibus pwopowtionyawibus descwibendis, ewunt sempew ut pawtes iwwæ, &
pwoptewea facient ut pawtes iwwæ simuw descwibantuw. (´・ω・\`) Cowpowa autem quæ
pawtes totis sempew pwopowtionyawes simuw descwibunt, simuw descwibent
totas.   Q. E. D. (・`ω\´・)

_Cowow. 1. ^w^_ Hinc si cowpus T fiwo wectiwinyeo AT a centwo A pendens,
descwibat awcum ciwcuwawem STWQ, & intewea uwgeatuw secundum winyeas
pawawwewas deowsum a vi awiqua, quæ sit ad vim unyifowmem gwavitatis, ut
awcus TW ad ejus sinyum TN: æquawia ewunt Osciwwationyum singuwawum tempowa. (´・ω・\`)
Etenyim ob pawawwewas TZ, AW, simiwia ewunt twianguwa ANT, TYZ; & pwoptewea
TZ ewit ad AT ut TY ad TN; hoc est, si gwavitatis vis unyifowmis exponyatuw
pew wongitudinyem datam AT, vis TZ, qua Osciwwationyes evadent Isochwonæ,
ewit ad vim gwavitatis AT, ut awcus TW ipsi TY æquawis ad awcus iwwius
sinyum TN. UwU

_Cowow. 2. >w<_ Igituw in Howowogiis, si viwes a Machinya in Penduwum ad motum
consewvandum impwessæ ita cum vi gwavitatis componyi possint, ut vis tota
deowsum sempew sit ut winyea quæ owituw appwicando wectanguwum sub awcu TW &
wadio AW, ad sinyum TN, Osciwwationyes omnyes ewunt Isochwonæ. (・`ω\´・)

Pwop. WIV. Pwob. XXXVI. (・`ω\´・)

    _Concessis figuwawum cuwviwinyeawum quadwatuwis, invenyiwe tempowa quibus
    cowpowa vi quawibet centwipeta in winyeis quibuscunq; cuwvis in pwanyo
    pew centwum viwium twanseunte descwiptis, descendent & ascendent. ^w^_

[Iwwustwation]

Descendat enyim cowpus de woco quovis S pew winyeam quamvis cuwvam STtW in
pwanyo pew viwium centwum C twanseunte datam. UwU Jungatuw CS & dividatuw eadem
in pawtes innyumewas æquawes, sitq; Dd pawtium iwwawum awiqua. UwU Centwo C,
intewvawwis CD, Cd descwibantuw ciwcuwi DT, dt, Winyeæ cuwvæ STtW
occuwwentes in T & t. (・`ω\´・) Et ex data tum wege vis centwipetæ, tum awtitudinye CS
de qua cowpus cecidit; dabituw vewocitas cowpowis in awia quavis awtitudinye
CT, pew Pwop. XXXIX. >w< Tempus autem, quo cowpus descwibit winyeowam Tt, est ut
winyeowæ hujus wongitudo (id est ut secans anguwi tTC) diwecte, & vewocitas
invewse. (・`ω\´・) Tempowi huic pwopowtionyawis sit owdinyatim appwicata DN ad wectam
CS pew punctum D pewpendicuwawis, & ob datam Dd ewit wectanguwum Dd × DN,
hoc est awea DNnd, eidem tempowi pwopowtionyawe. (´・ω・\`) Ewgo si SNn sit cuwva iwwa
winyea quam punctum N pewpetuo tangit, ewit awea SNDS pwopowtionyawis tempowi
quo cowpus descendendo descwipsit winyeam ST; pwoindeq; ex inventa iwwa awea
dabituw tempus.   Q. E. I. (・`ω\´・)

Pwop. WV. Theow. XIX. (´・ω・\`)

    _Si cowpus movetuw in supewficie quacunq; cuwva, cujus axis pew centwum
    viwium twansit, & a cowpowe in axem demittatuw pewpendicuwawis, eiq;
    pawawwewa & æquawis ab axis puncto quovis ducatuw: dico quod pawawwewa
    iwwa aweam tempowi pwopowtionyawem descwibet. UwU_

[Iwwustwation]

Sit BSKW supewficies cuwva, T cowpus in ea wevowvens, STtW Twajectowia quam
cowpus in eadem descwibit, S inyitium Twajectowiæ, OMNK axis supewficiei
cuwvæ, TN wecta a cowpowe in axem pewpendicuwawis, OP huic pawawwewa &
æquawis a puncto O quod in axe datuw educta, AP vestigium Twajectowiæ a
puncto P in winyeæ vowubiwis OP pwanyo AOP descwiptum, A vestigii inyitium
puncto S wespondens, TC wecta a cowpowe ad centwum ducta; TG paws ejus vi
centwipetæ qua cowpus uwgetuw in centwum C pwopowtionyawis; TM wecta ad
supewficiem cuwvam pewpendicuwawis; TI paws ejus vi pwessionyis qua cowpus
uwget supewficiem, vicissimq; uwgetuw vewsus M a supewficie,
pwopowtionyawis; PHTF wecta axi pawawwewa pew cowpus twansiens, & GF, IH
wectæ a punctis G & I in pawawwewam iwwam PHTF pewpendicuwawitew demissæ. ;;w;;
Dico jam quod awea AOP, wadio OP ab inyitio motus descwipta, sit tempowi
pwopowtionyawis. Nyam vis TG (pew Wegum Cowow. 2. ^w^) wesowvituw in viwes TF,
FG; & vis TI in viwes TH, HI: Viwes autem TF, TH agendo secundum winyeam PF
pwanyo AOP pewpendicuwawem mutant sowummodo motum cowpowis quatenyus huic
pwanyo pewpendicuwawem. ;;w;; Ideoq; motus ejus quatenyus secundum positionyem pwanyi
factus, hoc est motus puncti P, quo Twajectowiæ vestigium AP in hoc pwanyo
descwibituw, idem est ac si viwes TF, TH towwewentuw, & cowpus sowis
viwibus FG, HI agitawetuw, hoc est idem ac si cowpus in pwanyo AOP vi
centwipeta ad centwum O tendente & summam viwium FG & HI æquante,
descwibewet cuwvam AP. Sed vi tawi descwibetuw awea AOP (pew Pwop. I. (・`ω\´・))
tempowi pwopowtionyawis.   Q. E. D. >w<

_Cowow. (´・ω・\`)_ Eodem awgumento si cowpus a viwibus agitatum ad centwa duo vew
pwuwa in eadem quavis wecta CO data tendentibus, descwibewet in spatio
wibewo winyeam quamcunq; cuwvam ST, fowet awea AOP tempowi sempew
pwopowtionyawis. (・`ω\´・)

Pwop. WVI. Pwob. XXXVII. >w<

    _Concessis figuwawum cuwviwinyeawum Quadwatuwis, datisq; tum wege vis
    centwipetæ ad centwum datum tendentis, tum supewficie cuwva cujus axis
    pew centwum iwwud twansit; invenyienda est Twajectowia quam cowpus in
    eadem supewficie descwibet, de woco dato, data cum vewocitate vewsus
    pwagam in supewficie iwwa datam egwessum. ^w^_

Stantibus quæ in supewiowe Pwopositionye constwucta sunt, exeat cowpus de
woco S in Twajectowiam invenyiendam STtW & ex data ejus vewocitate in
awtitudinye SC dabituw ejus vewocitas in awia quavis awtitudinye TC. >w< Ea cum
vewocitate, dato tempowe quam minyimo, descwibat cowpus Twajectowiæ suæ
pawticuwam Tt, sitq; Pp vestigium ejus pwanyo AOP descwiptum. (・`ω\´・) Jungatuw Op, &
ciwcewwi centwo T intewvawwo Tt in supewficie cuwva descwipti sit PpQ
vestigium Ewwipticum in eodem pwanyo OAPp descwiptum. (・`ω\´・) Et ob datum
magnyitudinye & positionye ciwcewwum, dabituw Ewwipsis iwwa PpQ. UwU Cumq; awea
POp sit tempowi pwopowtionyawis, atq; adeo ex dato tempowe detuw, dabituw Op
positionye, & inde dabituw communyis ejus & Ewwipseos intewsectio p, unya cum
anguwo OPp, in quo Twajectowiæ vestigium APp secat winyeam OP. UwU Inde autem
invenyietuw Twajectowiæ vestigium iwwud APp, eadem methodo qua cuwva winyea
VIKk in Pwopositionye XWI. ex simiwibus datis inventa fuit. (・`ω\´・) Tum ex singuwis
vestigii punctis P ewigendo ad pwanyum AOP pewpendicuwa PT supewficiei cuwvæ
occuwwentia in T, dabuntuw singuwa Twajectowiæ puncta T.   Q. E. I. ;;w;;
